prologus reyse toure high large longe day touchynge great might toure babell men yit call men fro ferre may haue therof sight surmountith tour werke thus bifall serpentes many great dragon callyd cheef habitacion noman dare se wickyd eyre corruption great space grete cuntre aproche nere merueylous dungeon venemous mansion orrible noman dare approche lyke mountayn byldyd roche men say hadde therto repeyre toure atteynith vnto sterres clere transendeth region eyre stone syment made mater ioynynge stedfaste entier though fyre water dyd asseyle lytyll nought power shulde avayle made mighty endure well assuryd disposicion worlde lyuynge creature sawe neuer none lyke comparison whoos rerynge vp cheif occasion rich masonrie thrugh nembrothe pryde surquedie demyd proudly auice transcendyd noblesse thought moste mighty wy e felowe god lyknesse god worldely pride oppresse make prince eclypsen glorie suche trust thynges transitorie lorde eternall might toure nembroth lyste edifye made thondre levyn light therof fall full great partye boistous wyndes rage skye goddes power syde bygan thus abate perrell pryde discente fallynge stonys werkmen full many man dede oppressyd backe broken bone masonrye blode rede yit proud nembrothe werke hede thies sygnes lorde lyst nat knowe pompe brought ful lowe errour procedith furth newe thought wolde gete self aname melancoly chaunge loke hewe beganne also tempte atame encreas magnify fame newe toure edifye ayen lyke god ben blynde nothynge seen wolde haue raught vp sterrys seuyn thassent first counseyle robbyd god raught yn presumith lorde aboue tassayle reason shulde auayle prynces may well ayenst cry loude powere may elipse cloude myddes grete emprises proude nembroth makynge mason cumpas cast deuises geometry diuisions god hath aspeccious seynge thententis euery erthly man moste mighty best ayenst malice make resistence worldly power dominacion vengeable moste magnificence chastyce ouir whelme downe pryde prince euery region ensaumple nembrothe ye shal whose pompe raught aboue sterres clere whanne werkmen stode avantage moost besy intencion byfore tyme spake one langage sodenly transmutacion tonges made diuision wyrkynge obreyde man wist saide lykly accordynge reason chaunge made langages hertys made diuision bothe wyll corages ascendynge worchynge stage chaunge brother vnto brother lyke straungers noon knewe thentent myne auctour trowith aduersite ther gilt causyd vengeaunce elles god right equyte disposith hath ordenaunce amonge theym greate vareaunce thurgh worlde shulde theym self diuide nembroth disseuer nat abyde ganne anone amonge theym self disdeyn accepte nembroth theyr kynge monge forsoth nat tweyne another clere knowynge neither spech knewe pleyne menyng cuntre sennaar forsoke e theym asundry cuntre toke yd made lenger space folowyng fortune diuision beganne chefe theym newe dwellynge place tyes many aregion thus nembroth pryuyd put doun babell myghty famous toure callyd lenger possessoure ayenst pride nembroth frowarde fortune gan cours varye god also maner wroth surquedie contrarie place wilde solitarie sennaar furious sauage nembroth gan feble falle greate age yit sume bokes specifie waxe frowarde condicion first grounde ydolatrie fynder vp false religion causynge people haue opinion goddes worship paynymes wyse founder rightes false sacrifice towarde perce chees dwellynge place cuntre orient lordship shulde stretche greate space boundyd occident perce lande hath extent towarde party rede see londe perce list se bochas olde remembre put mynde howe perce costith enuyron septemtrion greate ynde many myghty region nembroth hadde first dominacion extedith bokes specifie oute mede garmanye lordshippes myn auctour saith withoute vertue ther true gyde theym suraunce none ne faith thinge passith may abyde wherfore bochas aspyte pride rebukynge folkes proude makynge compleynt crieth full loude pan exclamacion bochas ayen proude men shewynge howe god may theym pride wha best lift magnifye ayest heuyn holde champartye bildyth vp castelles reyse theym vp hight ademantys yron stronge ybounde square stonys large huge hight reyse vp youre walles moost myghty profound shyt dungeon castigacion fyndeth mekenesse repentaunce mercy maistresse ordinaunce ye ben wise considereth howe rote vicis pryde ye may well se pullith downe puttith vnderfote takyth counsell humilite ye lyst stonde suretie byldeth herte sekernesse toure vertues groundyd mekenesse whose masonrie costage vertues grounde souerayne lastys wyndes wedres rage neither tempest hasty ne sodeyne pompe ne blast though peyne vertue mekenes vndermyne feble make inclyne mekenesse groundyd verely though sumtyme fele aduersite ssith ouir suffrith pacientely venquisshith maner enmite assaute also contrariosite folowe consolacion whan sterne wyndes blastys haue layde lowe name mekenesse shall shewe wel knowe may trowblyd ouircome neuir tyme may suffre wer e ende venquisshith euir londe see whedre nere fe puissaunce constable myghty kynge callyd ia yn ordenaunce vpon iewys vengeaunce delbora gan prudently entende iewys tie wisdome diffende barach hir husbonde anone right neptalym ten thousande take wombe processe dyd aryse kynge glad also desirous childys state knowe sum wise thought wolde go sacrifise vnto appollo haue knowlechynge forne touchinge childe whan borne shulde folowe conclusion desirous hasty se first heuenly disposicion fauoure wolde appollos myghty deite haue answere amonge wittys childe fate shulde bifalle answere thought contrarye desire yit thus dede appollo tolde list lengre tar childe shulde verrely dede sle fadre make side blede handes none weye swerde must nedis deye kynge heuy trust sentence sorowfull herte god wote thynge fayne kest afore prouydence sonne shulde hast slayne wolde nat houre delayne birth bad men goon forest sle childe anone lyke byddynge mynystres wrought dede takynge childe tendre yonge age forest theym gan lede deuouryd bestes moost sauage moder ala almost fyll rage seynge childe inly fayre face shall thus dede dyde trespace lytell wondre though felt sm rte wymen reporte vnto moders tendre hert mater iugis nat ruth nat pite princesse quene allas shulde knowe hir childe deuouryd caas birth layus toke good kepe without mercy respite delaye vnto one kept shepe yonge childe vpon certeyn daye shall deliuered haste may entent myght nat socouryd shulde bestys deuouryd saide shepeherde goth forth anone right childe benygne beholdynge loke face thought herte inwarde sight shulde doo god greate traspace sle childe wherfore dyd grace toke first knyfe dyd besy peyne oute fete make hole tweyne toke small rod ayonge o e percyd fete ala pite bonde fast good leiser yonge childe henge vp tre entent ne shulde wilde bestes cruell sauage sodenly deuouryd rage vpon tre henge thus bounde auenture sum occasion straunge sheepherde hath childe founde ruth pite toke doun bare home toun made wife hir peyne fostre childe hir brestys tweyne whan brought forth recuryd full made hole woundes sore yonge childe hath enduryd whan age began wexe nature began rostore seide sheepherde louyd best hurtys edippus dyd calle edippus seyne conceyueth exposicion fete cyd throughout tweyne langage made mencion meropa wife kynge polibo sheepherde full humble entent began childe full lowly present bareyne nature kynge one affection toke edippus ure son heire adopcion reyne corynth succession kynge quene corinthe cuntre hadde childe greate cheerte let men considre discrecion sodeyne chaunge euery maner thynge childe sent oute distruction nowe prouydyd kynge fortune ay double werkynge refuse bestys moost sauage nowe receyued knyghtly herytage destitute kynrede forsake abiect blode allie tendre youth fete made blede henge tree began helpe crye god myscheef magnefie reconfort lolke disconsolate hathe made childe nowe thus fortunate prouydyd kynges heire stode deth auenture fortune shewe hir self foule faire folkys fressh corage auenture fell sothenesse ther strife su frowardnesse con e knowlechynge howe nat son vnto kynge discent b fer foreyne wherupon full sore bygan muse knowe put certeyne thought wolde sum maner practik vse kynge gan self excuse tyme withdrawe presence tyll knewe sum experience sum signe howe mater stode thought wolde diligence knowe fader also blode descendyd haue sum euydence saide edippus first thebe borne sent forest deuouryd founde brought forth ye haue herde forne drawynge home cuntre slough fader infortunate frowarde happys folowynge lyue tragedye fortune shall discriue high prudence vnto serpent declaryd euerydele slough knyghtly violence wisdome armure stele stace thebe tell full wele one cause yelist seen wherthrough edippus weddyd hath quene callyd iocasta princesse cuntre owne modre vnknowen though right faire vpon se mariage goddes full wrothe aliaunce nature gan loth moder ye shall vnderstonde shulde sonne take husbonde therein none conuenience supportyd kynde ne reason heuenly influence disposid inclinacion sum fals frowarde constellacion causyd saturne mar frowarde sterre engendre debate mortall werre mater pleyn thus deme cunnynge opinion though crownyd ceptre diademe regne thebe stronge myghty toun aspecte cam heuyn doun infortunate frowarde full rage ayenst kynde denyed mariage crownyd assent toun flourynge ceson ymeyne right faire vnto see quene iocasta myght gladder remembre whan wexe age goddes encreasyd linage hir ioye felicite se child inly faire oft ioye comyth aduersite hope vnsured whan hope oft apaire contrarious trust woll gladly repayre fals wenynge herte conceyued ignorance many folk haue disseyued thinge erth disceyuable whan man supposith verrely prosite stonde stable ioye remeuyd sodenly doolfull endure frowarde fate lokes browne kynge yre cast away crowne bigan race constreynt peyne hede wofull iyen tweyne day nyght cryed deth hatefull come mannys sight moost desirous yelde vp breth grace fals couetise eche tye desirous dede fore reigne succede thus bretherne moost infortunat betwene theym self fill discenceon finally vnkyndly debate brought thebe distruction zit made first conuencion enterchaungynge eche shulde reigne yere tother absent play come nere concludyd assent acorde region pollicenes rood forth abssent ethiocles toke first possession whan yere reuolacion come aboute fals entent vnto accord denyed assent cause striues pollicenes thus put oute right tyll adrastus kynge argyues thurgh grece gretest myght sent vnto thebe tedeus knyght sone lawe trete matere yere fully comme false frowerdly gan varye ethiocles conuencion adrastus lenger wolde tarye whan tedeus hadde made relacion callyd anon throughoute region worthy bothe nere ferre ayenst thebe forto kyngdome truly deuyse shuld haue detyd right betwene v tweyne ayenst truth dyd ordeyne besile region self alone haue possession yit hert cast another wyle vndoynge disolacion place dyde exile vnder thinge shulde oure loue deuyde one wyll one entencion lede oure life withoute diuision vnto goddes sum obseruaunce accord humble sacrifise made ministres feithfull attendaunce waite best wise nedith nat tell ne diuyse neither writynge bokes set halfe ioye made whan met first howe frendly dyd enbrace hertely gladnesse within armes tweyne howe ioye terys face full enteerly gan distyll reyne tye oude nat restreyne must frendship fraternall wepe dyd estate riall wily wolfe cast deuoure sely lambe diffence ne none helpe self socoure feble make resistence demyth truth fals apparence wondre fraude nat conceyuyd though lambys vnwarely disceyuyd though rose mydsomer full sote yit vnderneth hyd full sharpe spyne sum fressh floures haue full bytter rote lothsum gall also sugre vndermyne dredfull stormes sune amonge doth shyne wnder shadowe feyned frenlihede frendship perilous drede thus remembrynge feithfull wordes stable brother shewyd vnto oure metynge kyssynge amyable assuryd couenauntes oure fraternyte oft tyme men may beholde se lilyes growen amonge netles thicke floure delice myddes wedys wicke thus restyd kynges hous thinge aduertynge dedely crueltie olde hatred dede withoute obstacle sonne heuyn shewyd myracle sore agrysyd myght nat beholde bemys theron cast sight displesaunce cleernes began witholde vengeaunce withdrawe light day tournynge horrour nyght whan shone brightest mydday spere shroudyd face wold nat appere ala vpon caas horrible coude nat ymagyne neyther thynke mater odible get flessh th r blode also dyde drynke sore doth myn herte synke may nat touchinge auenture circumstaunce constreynt discure nedith nat make rehersaile touchynge myn exyll maner thynges diuers sorowes dyde assayle wofull sighes ne greuous wepynges neyther vpon nyghtes dolorous wakinges pouert neyther howe stode drede lese lyfe wherof bochas take hede remembre cyrcumstaunce euer thou sawe highe lowe degre contrarie vnhappy chauncis thou herde remembred weye balauncis sorowes let se sorowe myscheef vnrecuryd may countirpeyce haue enduryd myn enfortunes fonde theym ay fell without fauour socour dispurueyed brother euer cruell full oft desired haue dyed day sprite hath conueyed sorowe woo deuoide refuge wherfore praye bochas iuge thy wrytynge leue nat behynde neyther thy book thou nat disdeyne amonge folke thou haue mynde sorowe wepe weyle pleyn thus iohn bochas began aproche nere lyke fallen rage furiously abreyde langage howe may like man wode stes hath venym sowe abrood like ribaude falsly accusyd nat withstondynge full cleerly se myn infortunys may nat refusyd sore ala werke ayenst though estes fals vntrue vnto bochas face pale ayenst hath forgyd tale effect shall founde vntrue haue compleynt declare purpose tell tale newe fro bochas wherof toke gode hede blacke habyte torne wede sonne melliager hight erth none feirer se right well fauouryd euery men sight fynde natiuite present fatall sustres thre rockes bigan forto spynne prouyde meane weye saue cuntre last condescendyd melliager lusty corage shuld chefe folkes fressh yonge age dredfull boor mightely enchace furth went echon deuoide drede rounde speres gan manace meliager made first sydes rede swerde smote hede wherof cuntrye glad fayne wyse tusky bore slayne sume bokes tell huntynge lady borne arge callyd atthalonta doughter kynge sle bore toke charge arowe made woundes large also ouide like founde bycause yaue first wounde melliager anone memorye owne chosyn knyght yaue hir hede tokene victorye tw ne vncles ayenst skyll right raft hir hede force land fatall purueaunce kepyth cours sum clerkys sayne wrytynge doctoures substaunce deuines reply agayne afferme opinion vayne theym trust fate destyne god aboue hath soueraynte fortune power may restrayne helde longe euery tye stable tyll caught opinion sodeyn rancoure made vengeable hasty wrath nat commendable ayenst sone made honde chyst take fatell bronde sodenly cast fyre wexyd cruell ayenst womanhede execute hir venymous desyre fatall bronde amonge cole rede consumyd asshis dede furiously malencoly vengeaunce done thus gan cry ye parcas frowarde susters thre whiche ioue kepe lybrarye chyldren natiuite awayte sentence may varye wherso wilfull contrarye vpon dome takyng alway hede howe ye shall dispose fatall threde thou cloto takyst thy rocke hande lathesys doth bygynne great auise vnderstande threde lengthe drawe spyrine whan spirite shall body twynne thou antropos doest thy cruell peyne full frowardly parte threde tweyne may well playne deperticion day woo ala euer ye haue vntwynyd made diuision two brethern causyd theym disseuer lyue shall se neuer hast ala dyd auenge deth haue slayne son also ye doughters arberus felle whoos ougly modre blacke night kynred lynage lyue troylus wilfully forsoke hir nature quarell thus toke assaye nede also feyne take thirde leue theym tweyne passe ouer tell nomore neyther meany grekys wan toun howe eneas neither howe anthenore ayenst full woll rathest bright fethers pull ye haue warnyngys take hede ensaumple clere right visible howe worldly blis medlyd drede wittes resons sensible thinge seen ye nat incredible doctrine veyne tyme saue herof speciall preef whan dauid garnement caue mo tokyns ye lift haue another tyme dauyd also kepte life saul whan lay slept case hosteynge nat ferre asondre saul lay slepe people aboute slepynge vnpurueyed like flocke shepe whiche thinge dauyd toke good kepe doun descendyd made delay cam tent kynge saul lay spere saul stondynge hede dauid toke went way anone comynge man toke hede saul slept men echon whan vp hyll gone towarde saul ageyn cast loke made anoyse knyghtes woke first abnor prince chyualrye dauyd seyde wordes sentence abnor quod thou hast done greate folie day shewed greate negligence suffre saul magnificence peryll stonde none hede take aboute persone make knightes wal e thou art blame thy rechelesnesse leue kynge stonde greate drede slepe haue sauoure swetnesse life take hede negligence requireth mede deth turment rightfull iugement aboute prince whan folke negligent thou list se euydence howe life stode iudye se spere yeue therto credence howe vnprouyded ye youre tye saul thou ye may nat denye life deth youre power puissaunce day god put hole gouernaunce aquyte youre innocence euery man shulde vnto kynge declare none offence ageyn noblesse wyll werkynge god wote knoweth euery thynge neuer conspiracye wrouht compassyd ageyne regalye exaumple fight pacience ageyn malice shewe kyndnesse saul shewed mortall violence dauid aquit suffraunce goodnesse tyraunt venquesshyd prudent mekenesse men ageyn trouth may wele werre gynne ende palme doth ay wynne story ye take hede saul fall frowardnesse myscheef sodeyn drede philistees bible berith witnesse greate power gan wardys dresse vpon kynge saul auengyd tentys pight besyde gelboe wherof kynge saul astonyed herte lost sprite knightly hardynesse specially whan dyd aduerte prophete none army redresse future thynges trouth expresse israel cast greate drede bycause tyme samuell dede saul cast dyuynes israell eche dyuyneresse nat withstandynge palestynesse rys ageyn power oppresse ne knewe maner sorceresse myght counseyll take god tyme forsake wise stode disconsolate counseyl god prophete knewe none man moost infortunate vngraciously sped forth anone secrely saul forth gone woman shulde rede wysse israel callyd phetonesse whiche name clerkys writen office taketh hede soulis men ageyn clepe calle mene tofore dede thinge straunge rede wymen shulde lyst lere make soules dede men appere vnkouth straunge opinion wyt manere impossible nat accordynge semeth reson like thinge credible soule nature inuisible might appere shewe visibly vnto iyen bodely ferther flitte lest holde presumptuous deuynes mater comytte wise clerkes ben vertuous wittes subtill corious conclude doth theym seme mater trouth deme whether soule sconuell sprite dyd call tolde kynge israell bateyll shulde fall auentures myscheuys deth tolde also dede howe dauyd shulde succede bycause disobeysaunce writen rechelesnesse amelech toke nat vengeaunce thus sprite bare witnesse wherof saul fyll greteate heuynesse knowynge mene escape oute doute take fortune cometh aboute tolde also ennemyes wroth philistees beside gelboe batayle child shulde dye day necessite chiualrie shall scounfited regne lenger date god kingdome translate thus saul retournyd ageyn meny brought discounfiture whan sawe people slayne howe mene recure dedly wofull auenture bad squier take swerde blyue herte shulde ryue ennemyes vncircumcised shulde haue power story founde fall vpon haue deuysed yeue last fatall wounde high noblesse myscheef confounde squier fere god drede wolde nat assent foule dede slee lorde greatly aferde thinge hatfull euery mannys sight saul toke pomell swerde grounde full depe anone pight hast possible myght made poynt furious peyne perce herte part euen tweyne philistees anone dede spoilyd riall armure dismembryd smote hede tokyn disconfiture toke spoiles besy cure therof made best entent astraoth pride greate present thus saul slayne sentence philistees vpon gelboe forsake god inobedience abiecte also roiall fee thus lackynge humylite god euer set asyde lo ende surquedye pride lenuoye haue mynde saul estate riall lowe degre callyd makenesse presumpcion made haue fall god abiect frowardnesse lost crowne bible berith witnesse cause disobeysaunce goddys byddynge yaue none attendaunce god nat axeth nomore man atall hole herte without doublenesse giftys especiall yaue man high woldest leue thy mournynge restreyne thy importable woo sone shuldest thou se egall punysshinge vpon thy moost frowarde mortall foo warne shall nomore chastisinge fals auoutrie thy renoun right magnifye diffasinge thy true entent though youth vnbridelyd went large aforce cely innocent whoos wickydnesse ought bere charge right thy conscience discharge ioye vnlefull fals plesaunce double palme thyn honoure doth auaunce conceyue nd se thou lucrece howe reason good discrecion shulde thy trouble thy mournynge ceo right restreyne thy opinion rechelesly punycion knyf hande sle thy silf ala others gilt didest trespas latbe lucrece atbe thy dool cece thy complaynt thy woo restreyne shulde fro lyue alone fool thy deth petuelly compleyne put thy fader importable peyne oure welfare nat recheles dye leue childre moderles prudence eke thou oughtest se aduertise reason though force thy body corrupte thy soule inwarde thyn entencion fraunchisyd corrupcion offence none considre thyn infragilite woman hede haue hert stable thinge might comendable well know thou herte ay one fals lustys contrarie gouernaunce like image erued oute stone like woman flesshly plesaunce tyraunt fonde chere countenaunce euer womanly victorye shalbe ascryued thyn encreace glorie thy fader brutus hath well excused mysilf also thy blode thy kynrede mater late nomore musyd sle thy silf thy sydes blede certys lucrece thou hast full litell nede greate wronge oure iugement spare tyraunt sle innocent thy silf murdre sume wolde seme thou gilty thou art clene dyuers wittes diuersly wyll deme report thinge thou none didest mene thou shalt paciently susteene tyll thy chast wifly innocence may se punysshed violence folke wyll nat deme sone innocent wilfully whan nat culpable yildeth self deth iugement neuer afore gilt portable owne dome vpon self vengeable causeth people though report nought deme thinge neuer done ne wrought auengyd vpon thyn owne life excusynge thy dedly fame shewe thou art true weddyd wife wenynge deth gete name deuice thou art greatly blame thou yit knowest thyn honoure clerly shyne yeue people mater deuyne worde lucrece dyd abrayde full dedely loke chere theym ageyn euyn thus saide lathe husbonde lathe fader dere speke nomore matere lest men dempt hindringe name dred deth fals diffame youre counseyle shall life conserue sorowe sclaundre gladnesse lasse ill houre sterue euer languyssh sorowe heuynesse deth maketh ende worldly distresse saide sith full yore ago better dye euer lyf woo whan worship creature slayne dede sclaunderous report better deth dredfull peyne endure fals noise ay lif discomfort newe newe diffame hath resort neuer dyeth quickeneth outrage hatefull tunges venymous langage youre deuer halowe make stable chast chaumbres wifly gouernaunce case ye variable fals auoutrye vengeaunce shall folowe euerlastynge remembraunce howe true spousaile ye haue harde deuysed youre cite broke nat chastised ye founde case necligent punyssh auoutours right youre charge youre slouth ye assent luxuere vnbridelyd shall e abrode large shall youre conscience discharge woman stonde sekirnesse lucrece afforcyd clennesse dere husbonde ioye shulde thyn estate maner place like thy wife cherissh thyn armes goodly enbrace gilt horrible considered trespace tarquyn done ala welaway sone may neuer wasshed away fader myn howe shuldest thou call day thyn owne doughter dere ala refuce wymen thy plesaunce whilom moost entere within thy hous whan dyd lere clere exaumple manyfolde doctryne teyned vertuous discipline haue lost nowe dayes olde dispeyred recure ageyn myn owne childre dare nat theym beholde bycause wombe haue leyn diffoulyd pollute certeyn tofore chastite conseruyd chastise auoutre hath deseruyd part speke wordes fewe lenger lyue haue fantasie shulde face shewe dare appere company sith derke spot fals auoutrie shall euermore whether fals true myn hindrynge sclaundre renewe lust afforcid hath fals appetite freelte includyd nature maugre wyll foloweth delite sume folkys say euery creature good fame lost full harde recure sith may harmys nat redresse open gylt wyll confesse ageyn wyll oppressyd maner constreyned lust dede power might nat redressyd feblenesse stode greate drede offence deth shall mede sith leuer haue sume edge tole sle silf lyue slaundre dole fader myn spare haue pite dere husbonde rue myn offence goddys goddessys callyd chastite trespas graunt indulgence gylt make recompence venus gate vauntage deth shall redresse chastise myn outrage shulde make delay perce brest sharpnesse knife men wolde grueth force tresoure richesse hath ouer fortune dominacion kepeth hir euer vnder subieccion worldly folke rich apparaile lyue euer drede fortune wolde faile pore man afore theef doth synge vnder wodes fressh notys shyll rich man full feerfull robbinge ou kinge dred rideth forth ful styll pore large goth list wyll strongly fraunchised debate strif rich aferde alwey lose lif thus glad pouert hath palme wonne fortune outrayed hir doublenesse vpon pouert hast ronne streyned hir greate duresse tyll confessed playnly dyd expresse feith handem hir greate peyne abyde lawe pouert list ordeyne andiin hast disconfiture fortune began compleyne sore glad pouert thinge might endure charged fortune scorne hir nomore saide sith goo full yore reioyseth scorne folke veyne whan lothest shall scorned noyse comynge gan bete wynges vp anone aros marchus bedde lyinge gan tabrayde made tareynge toke harneys moost furious wroth wally haste goth cam first vpon wall force without tariynge doun tybre made theym haue fall felawys besy scalinge sheelde pauys ladder vp reisinge manly mark shortly comprehende flode made theym descende vnto deth abauyd knighthode hye renoun maugre theym capetoyle sauyd afterwarde rescued toun fortune conclusion tyme dyd vnto fall capitolinus men dyd call victorious lf alone hye victorye name gate hous perpetually memorye registred consistorye cronicles name determyned golden letter enlumyned gee whoom spake also well kept watch vpon night take offred vnto iuno solempnely greate torchys light also grauntyd ght whan famyne made store fa e sparyd take glad nowe heuy condicions folowynge fourme humanitees fals vsurped deytees nat sey saue drede flaterye wrongly erth dyd theym deifye eke alisaundre folowynge euer lust lordship greate might suffred dredes herte gan constreyne drede flode haue passage byhynde enmyes gan disdeyne liste slayne mortal rage fate approchynge yonge age towne pandosia tokyns dyd expresse acheronte bare therof witnesse dred bersanes quene wolde hir sonne auengyd tresons tofore wrought alisaundre lynage specially brought macedoyne hir auauntage hir sonne yonge age cassander thought dred haue tolde wolde auenge whan batailes nat ferre asondre though wylde storye seith sandrodoctus lept vpon syde backe beest tame towarde bateyle anone gan ryde capteyne day guyde robbours made mynde sloughe prefectys gentyll succession macedoyne mighty region title faders right hir herte gaue full greate gladnesse dempt none wight succede shulde haue none interesse fortune blinde fals goddesse disposyd child tweyne none theym purpos shulde atteyne whan fader lysymachus slayne sayde quene called arcynoe saue hir lif coude none gayne hir sonny feerfully fle cassander mighty stronge cyte ly drede one antigonus theym pursued story telleth thus brother quene arcynoe called ceramyus rescued hir partye ageyne antigonus ye may story se yi herte greate enuye albe nere one allye hir two sonny shulde kinges macedoyne regne cuntre sette couetise crowned macedoyne kinge fals treson story doth diuise theym desceyue werkinge first quene full humbly knelinge made promys vnder great surete macedoyne shulde crowned hir child faire visage shulde kept vnder gouernaunce vnto tyme come age put hir assuraunce ceramius swore god yeue sory chaunce purposed fals werkinge crowne hir quene make hir sonnes kinges toke goddys vnto witnesse swore ageyne pleyne visage vnto quene fraude doublenesse purpos haue hir mariage crowne hir quene hir greate auauntage thus sworne though hir brother yit herte god wote thought another vnder coloure assuraunce lete entre cassandre cyte cam ageyne plesaunce hir lordes hye lowe degre made stretys hangyd clothis golde solempne wyse goddys dyd sacrifise thus receyued solemply day halowed holde festyuall quene ioye ordeyned richely hir two sonny faire crowned crownes full royall goo afore hir maister strete gloriously vncle mete felonous herte vnder frendly face ceranius rote treson gan cosyns benigly enbrace purposinge fals collusion procede destruction finally first dyd peyne quene exyle sle hir child twyne treson brout preef whan quene apperceyued falsnesse sawe hir sonny brought mischeef coniured hir mortall distresse haue pyte naturall gentylnesse spare cosyns afore stode royall mercy nere borne blode crye passynge lamentable fyll afore swownynge vnto grounde lyke verely coupable seynge hir sonny bledynge many wounde nought mercy founde blode story nat feyned hir garnement doolfully desteyned hir face faire soyled ordure hir golden torne rent like thrall woofull creature mortall wepynge hir sight blent fynde howe sent burye hir child space yle called samontrace story maketh mencion princesse hye degre fonde greate cause lamentacion beynge doughter greate tholome hir child slayne vengeable cruelte beholde deth moost dolorous hir husbonde called lysymachus banysshed exile made hir ende sorowfull conpleynt hir lif thus drawe alonge tyll fate hir venymous purueaunce purposed afore outray theym thre child slayne knewe cheuysaunce moder exiled callyd arcynoe noble princis ware hye prudence amonge youre silf distaunce hyde rancoure hatfull violence vnder curteyne double daliaunce lyke herte shewe countenaunce vayde dissimulinge duplicite wysely wey chaptre balaunce lysymachus quene arcynoe howe ceramius macedoyne kinge murdryd cosyns hir fals traytoure vnkinde whoos treson made greate processe howe slayne batayle punysshed vengeaunce greate falsnesse lyke story maketh rehersayle remembre cast nat fayle folowynge myn auctoure hande boke doth specefie cam cuntre callyd pauonie folke gaule called fraunce conquere londys put theym silf prees moost notable peple puissaunce folowynge exaumple knightly encres ridynge worthy certeyne maugre tho wolde ageyne comon profyte drad nat dede cause fall age nothir put oute drede child lynage quaryll rightfull gaue auauntage herupon gadred newe knewe manly true purpose holde circuspecte auys theron made full prudent ordynaunce bellanicus olde hardy right wy afore prouided knightly purueaunce sayde tyraunt brought vnto mischaunce helpe assentyd vnwarly slayne whoos deth nat repentyd howe quene arcynoe auoutry done wt demetrius husbonde hir doughter beronyces ended sorowe story bochas gan applye turne penne like ye shall wryte telle frowarde lecherye arcynoe plesaut loke chere hir porte eke hir manere hir dayes like founde crafte beutye called venus secounde hir fairenesse youen mariage noble aga cyrenes kinge atwene yonge age doughter recorde writynge called beronices kinge endynge testament bad shulde wedded sonne kynge tholome done entencion cese werrys endured longe atwene egypt made mencion cyrenes bothe realmes stronge mariage might vnderfonge dyinge set fynall pe twene two realmes e icre who deth thus mater stode quene arcynoe moost subtyll werkynge ageyne mater cruell wode maryed hir doughter withoute lettinge called beronices ageyns byddynge hir fader called aga tofore rehersed ca maried hir one demetrius brother bochas rehersinge vnto mighty greate antigonus beynge grece macedoyne kinge infortunate hir weddynge story suynge ye shall se fals werkynge quene arcynoe conclude shortly matere whan quene double arcynoe sawe demetrius visage chere loke coloure langage beute manly porte liberalyte enamored hir flesshly fals plesaunce lyke hir desire haue aqueyntaunce hir nature moste lecherous hir frowarde inclynacion brought aboute demetryus assentyd hir suggestion accomplissh lyke hir opynyon hir desyres flesshly appetyte thus acorde cruell wyse offre vp men newe sacrifise bury quik bochas thus rede fals hope better spede fraunce grece toke ten noumbre half men wymen gedre tweyne tweyne fals murdre dyd encoumbre buryed theym quyk theyr deth full sodeyne sacrefyse goddys gan disdeyn ramayns wex contraryous fals rightys supersticious recorde olde croniculeers yere fyue hundre fro fundacion one twenty tho beynge consulers thre noumbre made mencion gouerned rulyd toun first called lucius emilius seconde catulus gaius actilius regulus thrid consulere senate ordeyned thre haue tolde selue yere gouerne rule cyte preserue aduersite ageyn two peples gaule lumberdye werred malyce enuye werre romayns stode boute senatours citeseyns bycause ageynst cam great route lumbardys halfe mounteyns ioyned togedre many fell foreyns stode departed made remembraunce fro rome obeysaunce people rude bestyall vnstable togedre assemblyd wode furious multitude innumerable vengeable herte corage despytous voyde reson sodeynly furious seyth bochas ferther gone soudiours bare gisarmys euerychon gysarmes gisarmes called towarde rome hastinge day day greate laboure fotemen sore app llyd ay truste multitude lay whoos comynge rome stode afray specially consuleers thre sent fight cite foure score thousand write croniclere mighty stonde diffence felawship eche consulere gisarmes noumbre sentence thre hundred thousande sturdy violence goynge fote finde eight thousand ouer feeld spred rekne nat rode horsbak six thretty thousand noumbre sixe hundryd ouer purposed wrak fynally romayns encoumbre shadowe gaue great vmbre soyle tofore grene enneth sonne shene capteyne abitomarus manly man full worthy knight went viridomarus another capteyne stele armyd bright twene romayns longe last fight party rome cite slayne consull one thre whoos deth fortune anone right party rome toun eyght hundred thousande toke flight thus began fame renoun abithomarus made mencion victorye herte made fayne partye thre thousand slayne romayns resorted agayn stronge batale feeld manly seyne proudly enmyes dyd assayle myn auctour maketh rehersayle gysarmys longe night fourty thausand slayne fight thrydde tyme help fraunce ioyned lumbardes folke gaule also faught ageyne oute ordenaunce beside ryuere callyd poo batayles togydre adoo fynde consulers tweyne romayn sheltrouns knightly dyd ordeyne maulius torquat called one flamynus flakkus ifere romayns forth gydre gon towarde ryuere full manly chere bataile story doth v lere nyne fourty thousand slayne day enmyes none ne went away abythomarus takyn prysonere tokne tryumphe brought rome toun capitoyle full pale chere led bounde chenys gayned raunson thus hath fortune appallyd hye renoun tokne disconfiture offred goddys cote armure thus lachesis lyues threde gan drawe tyll antropos brak full greate peyne viridomarus felawe slayn felde romayns certeyne worthy prince tweyne ende mortall fall feest accomplisshid callyd funerall tyme mortall werres atwene duke rome toun many toknes shewed sterres meruaylous lightnynges fro heuen doun many vncouth constellacion sondry cometes dyd walkinge appere seth storyes may trouth lere water pytene renneth itayle cuntre famous flode houre tyme batayle seith story turned blode fyres heyre moost furious wode mighty toures flamys brent thre monys apperinge orient peple fere fled lowe caues drede wex pale dedly chere thre dayes thre erth quauys duringe weres yere great appollo fyll doun pyllere marbyll white large great strength sixty cubites accoumted lengethe tyme story sayth nat nay rome consull great puissaunce callyd claudius slough vpon day thretty thousand brought mischaunce soudiours cam fraunce slayne many captayn lorne virydomarus spak toforne greate shame confusion remembryd scripture romayns made great oblacion vp iupiter cote armure tokne disconfiture within temple golde betyn clere despyte henge vp banere howe siphax munedye kinge take dyed prison bochas breuely remembraunce writeth werres debate batayles tyme itayle fraunce spayne chaupayne marciall apparayles amonge rehersayles telleth affrik great dissencion atwene hanyball worthy scipion toucheth name abydeth nat longe vpon storyes byde nat awhile nat rehersinge mighty werrys stronge stryues doth nat compyle doun dessendynge dyrecteth furth style reherce tell writynge fall siphax munedye kinge saide siphax batayles tweyne one kinge gabba might eke dyd payne mete masmissa anon right kinges put flight messulie fynde writinge howe masmissa gouernour kynge sayd siphax thrugh chiualrye made masmyssa fle region constreynyd lyue robbrye walke forestys bestys vp doun diffaute made mencion saue lyf fonde better refute fed silf rotys frute oute realme masmyssa enchasyd constreyned fle fro cuntre fro mynde folke name raced man wyste shulde liege men folke cyte affryk knewe better rede persone dempt dede thus kynge siphax encrece gan glorye force two kinges hath outrayed vpon wonne victorye put flight peple affrayed rome cartage dismayed eche theym dyd laboure werrys make gouernoure vnto siphax rome toun wretyn memoriall numedye sent scipion mater especiall cartage sent hastruball castell siphax lay tweyne arryued one day pleyne writinge haue conceyued story remembreth sentence cumynge receyued kinge shyhax greate reuerence notable manly diligence wretyn gode recorde made capteyns hertely acorde gedre lay night syphax greate suerte promyse made true knight nouther shulde deceyuyd founde greate duplycyte folowynge take hede lyke storye shall deuyse dede fraude falsnes moste mortall compassed beforn thus befall sleight hastruball affricans nye double vnder suger hide well gall hastruball fals decepcion vnder fayre chere desceyued scipion brought siphax fals subtylte sleyght peyntyd fayre langage shulde allyed full assente haue mariage sophanisba maydyn cartage doughter yonge faire withall seyth bochas hastruball thinge craft brought aboute accomplisshed verely dede mene pleynly doute first began rancoure hatrede symulacion feynyd falshede atwene siphax hastruball ala scipion diceyued ca done mariage syphax full enmye scipion hastruball rode cartage gan werraye agayn rome toun made mencion kynge masmyssa wildernesse towarde scipion haste gan dresse people gan make stronge helpe scipion bellius went ageyne syphax abode nat longe herte ageyne enuyous day story telleth thus affricans folkys cartage siphax romayns met visage masmyssa peple wode vpon siphax auengyd batayles cam stode maugre cruelte manhode space none fle brought home thrugh hye renoun hondys worthy scipion siphax take thus ware vnder baner maugre might rome led afore chare scipion noble worthy knight wan triumphe graunted right siphonisba afore sophax wif wed masmysse ende strif loo howe fortune chaunge hir tydes one nabyn full pytously wepynge tofore iohn bochas tyrannye macedoyne toke kinge hauynge title saue title robbrye force silf magnefye stronge honde toke full possession crownyd thilke region macedoyne floure hye clergye hye renoun moste famous souereyne marciall prowesse chiualrye gouerned londe newe pollicie stode kingdom auctours reherce kone amonge grekys lyke heuenly sonne laste eclipsed light macedoyne gan approch nere towarde argo nabyn dyd abyde entente abate pryde nabyn stode hyest estate grece liege debate duke callyd pilopomones people dwelled grece londe stryue nabyn put silf pres disconfited fightinge honde honde greate mischeef ye shall vnderstond alexamenes knight cuntre slough nabyn cronicle ye may se bochas reherceth mortall werrys betwene romayns affricans nabyn bochas doth procede tell warrys mortal stryues twene romayns affricans dede wherby full many loste lyues causyd wedowes maydyns eke wyues wepe weyle disioynt stode outher party se losse blode party rome toun notable tofore made mencion werres moost worthy moost able mene rome proude scipion cite cheuest champion entent affricans tanoye specially cartage destroye nye cartage ther cyte stronge mightely bilded stode vpon se wally thicke rounde square longe cheef diffence callyd cuntre saue kepe aduersite fourty cubites creestys marciall lyke fynde hight wall fronte reysed werre stonys square hye dungeon called birsa fro wonder ferre men might beholde cuntrees enuiron rede saluacion affricans purpos dyd ordeyne capteynes hastruballys tweyne sayde dungeon mightely batayled ageyn call sautys stonde endure worthy scipion hath nat fayled approch besy cure withe engynes mighty stronge sure force knight moost marciall great quantite brake doun wall lucius called sensoryne detyd marchus tyme bestyall tyll reson lawes constreyned vnder discrecion statutis naturall fro wylfull lustys prudence restreyned assente made one gydre encheyned golden cheynys pee vnite thus gan beeldynge euery greate cyte whan thou medlyst haue interesse one brynge discorde interupte thy doublenesse cite region one accorde lyke boke bere well recorde fro tyme thou first began thy mutabylite hath stroyed name forth lede boke furthre hir besynesse good roport yeue brightnesse laur ate stremys shad forth people foryetfulnesse neuer appalle bylle iohn bochas made vnto fortune full humble style whan fortune conceyued ca sobyrly stode gan stynt glad chere gan smyle myn auctoure fressh visage sentence spake langage hic loquitur fortuna sothly quod ise thy besynesse mortall men howe coryous howe studye greate auysnesse secretys preue knowe conceytys hyd within counseyles ye men youre peyne albe lightly ye may nat therto atteyne thys mater doth neuer feynt imagenynge likenesse youre mynde lyke youre conceytis ye forge men peynt sumtyme woman wynges set behinde portrayen iyen blinde cause breuely expresse youre owne couetous blyndnesse pyour appetytis moost straunge dyuers full euer chaunge doublenesse frowarde also malicious uers hasty climbinge worship richesse alweye voide trouth stablenesse moost presumptuous serche oute degree falsly tatteyne wordly dignitees bochas bochas ceyue euery thinge knowe full wele greate difference hyd thy silf wordys thinkynge atwene theym disconuenience hast thou nat wretyn many greate sentence thy boke sclaundre name hole entent maners diffame thou callest step moder moost vnkinde sumtyme fals chaunteresse mermayde tayle behinde scorne sumwhile namynge goddesse sumtyme witch sumtyme sorceresse fynder murdre deceitys thus malice mortall men call done despight accusacion many sundry wyse ye oft appech mutabylite namely whan youre requestys despise accomplissh youre gredy couetise whan ye faile ye lay wyte youre aduersitees falsly atwite thou purpos tesclaundre hast writen vngoodly contrarious fable howe wrestlyd glad pouerte whoos party thou fauourable settyst abak geyne thou vengeable nowe newe requeryst fauoure helpe furthre thy laboure skauns maners moost chaungeable condicions femynyne nowe nowe wynde vnstable thy descripcion thy doctryne euery chaunge redy enclyne wymen yonge tendre age nature diuers corage furthre tye thyn entent thy boke processe may procede fauoure accomplisshment well wyllyd helpe thy nede lyke thy desyre better thou shalt spede whan towarde benygne face spede thy iourney supporte grace thy name also thy surname poetys notable olde auctours may regest yd hous fame supportacion sodeyn fauours assistence also socours thy werke texplete laurer wynne saturnynus wyll thou begynne reherceth fortune hir condicions vnto bochas shewynge howe many one enhaunced tyme anone theym sodeynly ouerthroweth amonge romayns seyde saturnyne outragious condicion caused rome whan gan maligne greate debatys greate sedicious frowarde conspiracions sharpe enmy ageyne prudent iuge called metellus deuoyde refuge fro capitoyle set mighty hande fonde socoure metellus toun tyme thou shalt vnderstande howe myn helpe supportacion one smal reputacion called glabeya pouert brought lowe made consulere story well knowe seruaunt first almoost sette nought afterwarde made fortunate left neuer tyll brought prerogatyf chose senate pretoure office estate also wrought conspiracion bringe metellus destruction whoos assent also another called marrius beynge yere texplete thys treson owne sworne brother also tyme consulere fortune made full gode chere lyke desyres gaue liberte banissh metellus cite thre romayns first saturnyne glaucia called seconde marrius layde hoke lyne haue tolde metellus confounde purpos also founde fauourable brynge mischeef storye sheweth opyn preef banysshed rome toun saturnynus subtyll werkynge clambe vp fast presumpcion called rome lorde kinge gaue fauour manere fals smylynge tyll last playnly declare destruction brought snare senatours knowynge malyce saturne made greate gad rynge sundry folke castynge auyce fauoure might called kinge vp clymbynge shewed durynge longe space desceyue benygne face tyll marryus mighty consulere withstonde presumpcion rose stronghande aknightly chere beset pal y aboute enuyron brake gatys amyd toun saturnynus voide fauour capytoyle fled socoure forbarred marrius vitayle capitoile beseged rounde aboute entringe stronge bataile outher tye slayne great route thus fauour gan stonde donte thus saturnynys brought great distresse gode achetyd lost richesse experience full openly men bereth hyest therupon ascende lyke tourne whele requireth whan leest wene doun shall descende haue power silf diffende ageyne might whan ouerthrowe laugh make mowe rusus also borne great lynage descendyd full hye noblesse vnto vertue contrarye corage frowarde founde gentylnesse yit chose storye doth expresse questoure asya office degre byrth gouerne cuntre oft tyme vertue gentylnesse come nat heires succession exaumple drusus story bereth wytnesse corage disposicion euer frowarde condicion let men deme must nedys nat birth dedys vertues set aside slowe armed hated chiualrie moost couetous deynous full pryde dedys frowarde full trecherie hye estate dyd magnefie yit giftys ne might stre ch tofore cometh like wretch dare shame nat shewe visage ferre disclaundryd wretchydnesse who couetyse vicious outrage falsly caused doublenesse maguldusa prince greate noblesse betrasshed mede kinge called boccus drusus fals werkynge manere torment greuous peyne competent couenable condigne outwarde flater feyne herte couertly maligne drusus dyd shewed many signe maguldusa loue frendlihede vnderneth fals treson hyd dede maguldusa lak cause destruction contrarious mutabylite notable famous scipion tyme cynsoryn caton gate triumphe many greate victorye put name perpetually memorye merytes chose consulere cheef busshop gouerne greate tripet fro whele cast lowe doun moste hyest domynacion toke none hede dyd laugh mourne noman alwey soiourne bochas quod fortune take gode hede also howe disauayle exaumple se howe athenyo mene rome toun agaderinge greate cumpanye togedre sworne fals conspiracye withdrawe fro presence tribune called lodonce knighthode gouernaunce sent doun rome cyte mighty honde rule great cuntre called chaumpayne pleynly seye peple lyst nat obeye score foure theym noumbre named cheef conspyratours cast capteyn encoumbre multitude theuys robbours chase amonge theym supportours mighty capteyns one called spartharchus chefest echon gadred churles made silf stronge hye hyll toke dwellynge place hauynge rewarde right wronge spoyle cuntre bestys enchace cherisshed benigne face ceson gaue liberte fals rauyne robbe cuntre thinge cruell comparison vengeable wyll nat right whan chorle hath domynacion lak discrecion blindeth sight comuners defaute light whan haue power cuntrees gouerne fare lyke beste nothinge discerne gladiatores folkys dyd call swerdys steele made fyne fight geyn wylde bestys lyon beerys bore wylde swyne mounteyne dyd lyne called venuse cruelte slough robbyd eche cuntre spartharchus cheef capteyne brought vp nought borne lowe degre claudius mighty stronge romayn sent power fro rome cite diffende saue cuntre hyll besegynge afore lay rebuked bete dryuen away many kept mounteyne hurte day storye telleth thus amonges slayne greate capteyne felawe vnto spartharchus fynde hight ynomaus whoos deth take great vengeaunce cuntre felt therof greuaunce mounteyne one assent without mercy remission moost vengeable haue robbyd brent cuntre aboute enuyron tyll two consulers fro rome doun first called lentulus put flight seid spartharchus wherof romayns greatly dismayed senatours indignacion asshamed silf affrayed sent one crassus great lorde toun noumbre legion whan spartharchus first set slough men six thousande whan met afterwarde besyde great riuere called salaire greate batayle spartharchus stode greate daungere chere countenaunce gan fayle thretty thousande clad plate mayle slayne day geyned raunson capteyns assigned pryson without made mencion sixty imperiall cite hath ay ben redy equite besy also noblesse wronge tyrauntes manly oppresse philosopher poetys eke deuyse sawes prudent notable blode tyrauntes noble sacrifyse god aboue whan vengeable sith ye rightfull iust stable youre werkys voyde varyaunce weye matere iustly balaunce peple echon one assent outrage thys andronycus put doun rightfull iugement whoos place set vp isacius sayde tyraunte frowarde vicious gan maligne theym silf dresse diffence make forteresse holpe nat make resistence stode voyde fauoure syeged violence maugre might rent oute toure spoyled cruelly felt better socoure sode naked quakynge peyne first rent oute one iyen tweyne ouermore rewarde without helpe socoure respyte rode asse face set bakwarde assys tayle holdynge despyte beholde people hath delyte pore rich thrugh cite rebuke grauntyd lyberte carte set vengeably lad toun dome hanged hye gybet peple confusion made clamoure terryble soun wolde neuer fro galowes wende tyll mischeef deth made ende lenuoye tragedye ageyn audronytus bochas maketh exclamacion ageyn princys vicious haue power domynacion tyrannye vse extorcion concludynge thus fals lyuynge right requyreth haue euyll endynge indifferently tyraunt lecherous wyues maydyns made none excepcion folowynge luste frowarde disclaundrous spared woman religion made wyues breke profession violence peyse well thinge right requireth haue euyll endynge moost murdre contagious innocent blode make effusion vengeable also ageyn vertuous ageyns kinrede sought occasion sle fro cam doun consydryd fals werkynge right requyreth haue euyll endynge bochas manaceth princys outrageous proude hatefull abusion god man wyll contrarious hauynge herte fals opynyon tho subiection may deuoure power serchynge shall nat fayle haue euyll endynge noble prince ye desirous seuere youre domynacion vertue victorious cherissh trouth put falshede doun mercyable mesured reson andronytus surfetys shewynge ye grace may haue gode endynge isacyus made blynde taken myscheef reherced whan isacyus empyre possession auenge deth andronytus constantinople royall toun brother cam doun bacyn brennynge bright glede made blynde nomore rede except isacyus
